We think it‚Äôs fair to say that planning a wedding is one of the more stressful and trying things that a couple may go through. But once that day arrives and the hard work falls behind you, and all you‚Äôre left to do is stand in-front of your best friend and say ‚ÄúI do,‚Äù you realize every bit of it was worth it‚Ä¶ that for some odd reason... you want to go through it all over again. Which leads us to why the Twenty Mile House and its staff and vendors were beyond impressive!

First things first‚Ä¶ Rachel Mann. Our Coordinator, our advisor, our trusted leader through the wedding planning process. She simply made it easy. Her creativity, outstanding communication, firm guidance, organized file-sharing system, and overall calm, cool, and collected attitude on the wedding day, made us feel at ease. We knew if we forgot something, that Rachel had us covered. It‚Äôs the comfort she created that alleviated the stresses and permitted us to enjoy ‚Äúour day.‚Äù

The Twenty Mile House is a truly magical place‚Ä¶ especially at night when the moon and stars come out, the lights turn on, and then a 10-ton train comes barreling down the tracks, commemorating your moment with a blow of the horn. It‚Äôs the little (and big) touches around the venue that make all of the difference in the world. It‚Äôs having your dearest friends and family staying on-site with you for the entire weekend. It‚Äôs the friendly staff stopping to take a moment to say ‚Äúgood morning‚Äù and see how your day was going. It‚Äôs that feeling of appreciation you have for the people working tirelessly to setup and breakdown the ceremony and reception site, the bar and coffee stands, or to do the groundskeeping. It really is the people, combined with this beautiful site, that make it an amazing wedding venue.

One highlight for us was getting to attend the Wedding Fair. Wow, we had no clue when we picked the TMH that we would have so many vendor options! We were able to sample food by local caterers, listen to music from talented DJs and guitarists, preview table layouts and settings including floral displays, meet photographer/videographer teams, and spend a nice day walking the grounds and envisioning where things would go and how it may look on our day. We got married roughly 10 months after the Fair, but having had the chance to make many decisions early-on, especially on-site at the venue, allowed us to put together what we would say was a perfect day.

We would like to thank everyone involved:
The Twenty Mile House and its entire Staff

She guided us through the planning sheets, helped fill in important details, gave advise where we simply had no ideas, and was very responsive with her communication. She immediately helped us organize all our decorations and ‚Äústuff‚Äù upon arrival. During the rehearsal and day of, she provided much needed direction on the flow of the ceremony, and managed to keep everyone on track. She also took care of countless small, yet meaningful details that made my husband and I feel extremely well taken care of (for instance, bringing us appetizers/beverages during pictures to make sure we were eating!). She also clearly had a handle on the ‚Äúvision‚Äù for the decorations and theme. She even suggested a few additions that were quite stellar! The wedding (ceremony and reception) went off without a hitch ‚Äì EVERYTHING WAS PERFECT. We had to shuffle the schedule a bit, but the way it was managed by Rachel and staff was so fantastic and low stress. At the end of the night, she gave a heartfelt goodbye to me and my husband, left us food and champagne in our cabin, and told us to simply enjoy our night however long we wanted it to go.

The food was as amazing as Rachel. We went with Pangaea Cafe, led by head chef Holly. She had a delicious array available for us during our trial tasting, and was very flexible with tweaks we asked for (i.e. different topping options available depending on guests‚Äô dietary restrictions), and even accommodated the request for a popcorn machine and toppings bar! Everyone was raving about the food afterward; the stuffed mushroom and homemade salad dressings are of special note!

For dessert, we went with Quincy Cooking Cottage led by Connie. She let us sample (i.e. went out of her way to bake and/or save us pieces) some additional cake flavors and worked with us on personalizing the German Chocolate 8‚Äù cutting cake we landed on. We also had a dessert bar, complete with chocolate mousse, mini apple tarts, and a cheesecake bar with toppings. Everything was delicious! More ravings from guests, and we have most of a beautiful, decadent cake remaining to look forward to for a while ÔÅä

The flowers, provided by Sonia at Gray‚Äôs Flower Garden, were STUNNING. She absolutely NAILED the vision I was going for, including the most natural yet beautiful bouquet, appetizer/dessert table with moss, sprigs in napkins, and more. I kept as many arrangements as I could to preserve and keep around the house ‚Äì so pretty!

Todd with Lionsmile Entertainment was likewise fantastic. He played all the songs we‚Äôd requested on the playlist, mixed in some additional songs he knew would be good to get people to the dance floor, and even went out of his way to let us know how much he enjoyed some of the song selections. He was so easy to work with and genuinely loves what he does ‚Äì he did a great job with the announcements as well, and stayed with us late into the night!

Lastly, some words for the staff and venue itself. The staff were all incredibly helpful, nice, professional, and efficient. I especially remember one of the bar tenders (Jason) making sure the bridal party was taken care of, and left us with some options long after the staff had left. The property is even more beautiful in person than the pictures show, especially with all the personalized touches from our wedding. We had a bit of a windier/cooler day, but the staff turned on heat lamps, started fires, and made sure guests were comfortable.

Overall, a complete rave review for the Twenty Mile House!</text>

<text>Quality bikes in the middle of Santa Monica (not on the beach). < text>
This is the only poke place I go to in Pleasanton. I have tried others, and each time I've wished that I had just gone to this place. Prime Poke has a good option of fish to choose from, and the sauces are really good. I always order the two protein, because the three is too much for me, and I have always gotten the tuna for the free scoop, the marinated salmon, and the marinated tuna (I dont remember the exact name). For the last meat you order, they let you choose mix ins, I get the cucumber, cilantro, and serrano. Then for sauces my favorite for the mix ins in spicy poke and teriyaki. For the sauces on top, I would recommend sriracha and the spicy mayo, if you like spice, or just the spicy mayo if you want it to be mild. However, even with all that spicy stuff on top, it is not an overpowering amount of spice. I tried for the first a topping, I forget the name but I'll include a picture, and it was a good amount of crisp but the pieces were just a little too large for my taste. If you're in Pleasanton, and feel like poke, I would definitely try this place out!< /text>

This review is for my skeptics...
If you are reading this review more than likely you dont have perfect credit and little or no down payment but need a reliable car. Long story short I was a skeptic myself. Like you i read almost ever review before making my decision. I previosuly bought a car off craigslist and to no surprise it has stopped working. I needed a car ASAP to get around in. I didnt want to settle for anything so here I am. I bought my car Saturday and took it to Midas Monday for an inspection. My 2005 Nissan Exterra is in perfect condition inside and out. Midas stated that the only thing I need to have looked at is what they are calling a blend door actuator. This is not a problem except is makes a noise when the car turns on but it will do no harm if not bolted down. Outside of getting new tires I need NO work done and I am very grateful for that. The cars they carry are from 2000 to 2014 so please dont go in with the mindset that you will walk out with something new. This place is great for people with troubled credit or no credit and low down payments. Best part off it will be paid off in 2 years!!!  Thank you guys for selling me a great car :)
